  <script type="application/javascript">
   function search_popup1(){
	$('#search').hide();
	$('#overlay').remove();
}
  </script>
  <script>
   $( document ).ready(function() {
	$(".search").keyup(function(){ 
	var searchid = $(this).val();
	var key = searchid.length;
	if(key &gt;=2){
	//alert(key)
	var dataString = 'search='+ searchid;
	if(searchid!='')
	{
		$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		timeout: 1000,
		url: "http://www.myscorz.com/view/controller.php?action=getallsearchs_top",
		data: dataString,
		cache: false,
		success: function(html)
		{
		$("#result").html(html).show();
		}
		
		});
	}return false;    
	}
	});
	jQuery("#result").live("click",function(e){ 
		var clicked = $(e.target);
		console.log(clicked);
		var show_name = clicked.attr("class","show_name").html();
		var decoded = $("&lt;div/&gt;").html(show_name).text();
		$('#searchid').val(decoded);
		jQuery("#result").fadeOut(); 
	});
	jQuery(document).live("click", function(e) { 
		var $clicked = $(e.target);
		if (! $clicked.hasClass("search")){
		search_product1();
		jQuery("#result").fadeOut(); 
		}
	});
	
	$("#searchid").toggleClass("blue-placeholder");
	$(".search-txt").toggleClass("home-placeholder");
	
});
  </script>
  <script type="application/javascript">
   function search_popup2(){
	
	var postData = $('#noprofile').serializeArray();
	var a = postData[0].value;
	if(a!='')
	{
	$.ajax({
		type: 'POST',
		url: 'http://www.myscorz.com/view/controller.php?action=noprofile',
		data: postData,
		success: function (data) {
			console.log(data);
			if(data ==1){
			$('#search').hide();
			$('#overlay').remove();		
			}
		}
	});
	
	}
}
  </script>
  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){
	$('#personal').hide();
	$('#product').hide();
	$('#business').hide();
});
function radio1(){
	$('#personal').show();
	$('#product').hide();
	$('#business').hide();
	
}
function radio2(){
	$('#personal').hide();
	$('#product').show();
	$('#business').hide();
	
}
function radio3(){
	$('#personal').hide();
	$('#product').hide();
	$('#business').show();
	
}
function profile_submit() {
	
	var postData = $('#profile_sub').serializeArray();	
	var a = postData[0].value;
	if(a ==''){
		$('#first_name_error').show();
	}
	if(a!='')
	{
	   $.ajax({
		type: 'POST',
		url: 'http://www.myscorz.com/view/controller.php?action=profile',
		data: postData,
		success: function (data) {
			if(data ==1){
				$('#content').hide();
				$('#success_msg').show();
			}
		}
	  });
	}
		
}

function product_submit() {
	var postData = $('#product_sub').serializeArray();	
	var a = postData[0].value;
	if(a =='') {
		$('#first').show();
	}
	if(a!=''){
		$.ajax({
		type: 'POST',
		url: 'http://www.myscorz.com/view/controller.php?action=product',
		data: postData,
		success: function (data) {
		if(data ==1){
				$('#content').hide();
				$('#success_msg').show();
			}
		}
	  });
	}
}

function business_submit() {
	var postData = $('#business_sub').serializeArray();	
	var a = postData[0].value;
	if(a =='') {
		$('#1').show();
	}
	if(a!=''){
		$.ajax({
		type: 'POST',
		url: 'http://www.myscorz.com/view/controller.php?action=business',
		data: postData,
		success: function (data) {
			if(data ==1){
				$('#content').hide();
				$('#success_msg').show();
			}
		}
	  });
	}
}
  </script>

  <script>
   function ask_login(name){
		var msg_content = "";
		var overlay = $('&lt;div id="overlay"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
		overlay.show();
		overlay.appendTo(document.body);
		var url = default_url+"/login/";
		var login = "&lt;a href='"+url+"'&gt;Login&lt;/a&gt;";
		if(name == "compare"){
			msg_content = "Please "+login+" to Compare";			
		}else if(name == "follow"){
			msg_content = "Please  "+login+" to Follow";
		}else if(name == "message"){
			msg_content = "Please  "+login+" to Message";
		}else if(name == "score"){
			msg_content = "Please  "+login+" to Score";
		}else if(name == "where_to"){
			msg_content = "Please Contact us for Affiliate Marketing Opportunities";
		}
		
		
		$('#login_msg').html(msg_content);
		$('.login_popup').show();
		$('.close').click(function(){
			$('.login_popup').hide();
			overlay.appendTo(document.body).remove();
			return false;
		});
		$('.x').click(function(){
			$('.login_popup').hide();
			overlay.appendTo(document.body).remove();
			return false;
		});
	};
  </script>
  <div class="login_popup" style="display:none">

     <div class="head-tit">
      <h3>
       Details
      </h3>
     </div>
     <p>
      Leonardo Wilhelm DiCaprio (born November 11, 1974) is an American Actors and film producer. He has been nominated for five Academy Awards and ten Golden Globe Awards. He won the Golden Globe Award for Best Actors in a Drama for The Aviator (2004) and the Golden Globe Award for Best Actors in a Musical or Comedy for The Wolf of Wall Street (2013). He has also been nominated by the Screen Actorss Guild, Satellite Awards, and the British Academy of Film and Television Arts.
     </p>

  <script>
   $(function() {
		$("#example-one").organicTabs();
		$("#example-two").organicTabs({
			"speed": 100,
			"param": "tab"
		});
	});
	var rootUrl = "http://www.myscorz.com/functions/updatescore";
	var productID = '1229';
	//alert(rootUrl);
	var getScore = function(){
		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			url: rootUrl,
			data: {method:"UpdateScore",prod_id:productID,user_id:""},
			success: function(response) {
				//alert(response);
				$("#MyScore").text(response);
			},
			error: function(msg) {
				//alert(msg);
				console.log("fail");
			}
		})
	};
	setInterval(function(){getScore()},10000);	
	function change_ratio(org, upd) {
		/*var diff, result;
		// increase of percentage

			diff = org - upd;
			result = (diff/upd)*100;
		} else if(org &lt; upd) {
			diff = org - upd;
			result = (diff/org)*100;
		}
		alert(result);*/
	}
	$(document).ready(function() {

	});

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var data = "";
function crop_img_fn() {
//alert("hai");

$( '.cropimage' ).each( function () {
var image = $(this),
cropwidth = image.attr('cropwidth'),
cropheight = image.attr('cropheight'),
results = image.next('.results' ),
x = $('.cropX', results),
y = $('.cropY', results),
w = $('.cropW', results),
h = $('.cropH', results);
//download = results.next('.download').find('a');
 
image.cropbox( {width: cropwidth, height: cropheight, showControls: 'auto' } )
.on('cropbox', function( event, results, img ) {
x.text( results.cropX );
y.text( results.cropY );
w.text( results.cropW );
h.text( results.cropH );
data = img.getDataURL();
hideLoading();
//download.attr('href', img.getDataURL());
});
});
};

function showLoading(){
document.getElementById("loading").style = "visibility: visible";
}

function hideLoading(){
document.getElementById("loading").style = "visibility: hidden";
}

function showMyareaLoading(){
document.getElementById("myarea_loading").style = "visibility: visible";
}

function hideMyareaLoading(){
document.getElementById("myarea_loading").style = "visibility: hidden";
}

function showme(){
	document.getElementById('bg_div').style.display="block";
	document.getElementById('FlashID').style.display="block";
}

function hideme()
{
	//hideMyareaLoading();
		document.getElementById('bg_div').style.display="none";
		document.getElementById('FlashID').style.display="none";
}	

$(document).ready(function()
{
$('#myarea_img').live('change', function()
{
showMyareaLoading();
$("#popup_gal").html('');
//$("#popup_gal").show();
//$("#popup_gal").html('&lt;img src="loader.gif" alt="Uploading...."/&gt;');
$("#imageform").ajaxForm(
{
target: '#popup_gal',
success: function(res) {
hideLoading();
showme();
crop_img_fn();
 //alert("hai");   
}
}).submit();

//crop_img_fn();
//setTimeout(function(){crop_img_fn()}, 9000);
});

function download(){
	showLoading();
	var post_url = "http://www.myscorz.com/crop_image/";
	var img_name = $("#pro_img").val();
	$.post(post_url, {
	imageData : data,
	image_name: img_name
}, function(data) {
	//alert(data);
	
	hideme();
	var thumb = "&lt;img style='height: 110px; width: 100px;' src='http://www.myscorz.com/uploads/products/thumb/"+img_name+"' /&gt;";
	$("#preview").html(thumb);
	$(".main_upload").val(img_name);
	//window.location = data;
});
}

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(".scroll").click(function(event){
		 event.preventDefault();
		 //calculate destination place
		 var dest=0;
		 if($(this.hash).offset().top &gt; $(document).height()-($(window).height())){
			dest=$(document).height()-$(window).height();
			dest=dest-110;
		 } else {
			dest=$(this.hash).offset().top;
			dest=dest-110;
		 }
		 //go to destination
		 $('html,body').animate({scrollTop:dest}, 2000,'swing');
	});
	function doreview(rev,id,user_id,prd_id) { 
		var param = { rev:rev,id:id, user_id:user_id, prd_id:prd_id};
		$.ajax({
			url: 'http://www.myscorz.com/doreview/',
			type:'POST',
			data: param,
			dataType:'html',
			success: function(result) {
				//alert(result);
				if(result==1)
					window.location.reload();
				else if(result==0)
					alert("Unable to review,try again");
				else if(result==2)
					alert("You already have reviewed this comment");  
			}
		});
	}
	
	function do_view(user_id,prod_id) { 
		var param = {  user_id:user_id, prod_id:prod_id};
		$.ajax({
			url: 'http://www.myscorz.com/do_view/',
			type:'POST',
			data: param,
			dataType:'html',
			success: function(result) {
				if(result==1)
					window.location.reload();
				//else
					//alert("Unable to review,try again");
			}
		});
	}	
	
	function do_follow(id,status) { 
		var param = { id:id,status:status};
		$.ajax({
			url: 'http://www.myscorz.com/do_follow/',
			type:'POST',
			data: param,
			dataType:'html',
			success: function(result) {
				if(result==1)
					window.location.reload();
				else if(result==0)
					alert("Unable to follow,try again");
			}
		});
	}
	function compare_people(id) {
		var count=$("#compare_count").val();
		var id = id;
		var formData = {action:"docompare_people",id:id}; //Array
		$.ajax({
			url : "http://www.myscorz.com/view/controller.php",
			type: "POST",
			data : formData,
			success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
				$('#comparition_width').append(data);
			},
			error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) { }
		});
	}
	function compare_product(id) {
		var count=$("#compare_count").val();
		var id = id;

				$('#comparition_width').append(data);
			},
			error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) { }
		});
	}

		onchange: function (value, text) {
		$("#sub_cat_"+value).show();
		if(value==1) {
			$("#sub_cat_2").hide();
			$("#sub_cat_3").hide();
			$("#sub_cat_4").hide();
		} else if(value==2) {
			$("#sub_cat_1").hide();
			$("#sub_cat_3").hide();
			$("#sub_cat_4").hide();
		} else if(value==3) {
			$("#sub_cat_1").hide();
			$("#sub_cat_2").hide();
			$("#sub_cat_4").hide();
		}else if(value==4) {
			$("#sub_cat_1").hide();
			$("#sub_cat_2").hide();

	function delImage(id,table,page_id)

{ 

var r=confirm("Are you sure you want to delete image?");

	if (r==true)

  	{ 

var param = {table:table, id:id, page_id:page_id};

$.ajax({

  url: 'http://www.myscorz.com/do_deleteImage/',

  type:'POST',

  data: param,

  dataType:'html',

  success: function(result) {
	if(result==1)

	window.location.reload();

	else

	alert("Deletion Failed Please Try Again");

	  

  }

});

}

}
